      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses that will occur in the 30th century
       </b>
       . During the period 2901 to 3000 there will be 248
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 91 will be partial, 82 will be annular (two
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 64 will be total, and 11 will be hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year will be five, in 2904.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div style="clear:both;">
